# Animal Fat

# Description __

Harvested from animals, combine with cloth to create a low quality fuel source.

Page views: 5,321  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Stone Fireplace

# Description __

A stone fireplace to heat your home. Must be placed indoors and against a wall.

Page views: 6,949  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Champagne Boomer

# Description __

A very large mortar type firework with an massive champagne colored explosion followed by smaller orange starbusrts

Page views: 3,659  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Green Boomer

# Description __

A very large mortar type firework with a green starburst

Page views: 2,880  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Orange Boomer

# Description __

A very large mortar type firework with an orange starburst

Page views: 2,654  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Red Boomer

# Description __

A very large mortar type firework with a red starburst

Page views: 3,672  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Violet Boomer

# Description __

A very large mortar type firework with a violet starburst

Page views: 2,612  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Blue Roman Candle

# Description __

A small repeating firework, shoots a series of Blue balls into the air

Page views: 3,233  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Green Roman Candle

# Description __

A small repeating firework, shoots a series of Green balls into the air

Page views: 2,544  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Red Roman Candle

# Description __

A small repeating firework, shoots a series of red balls into the air

Page views: 2,540  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Violet Roman Candle

# Description __

A small repeating firework, shoots a series of Violet balls into the air

# Survival Fish Trap

# Description __

Traps fish, place on the shore and load with bait. The more bait loaded the bigger the chance of catching Trout.

Page views: 5,851  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Flame Thrower

# Description __

A Flamethrower useful in destroying wooden buildings. Uses low grade fuel as ammunition. Not terribly effective in PvP.

Page views: 9,094  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Flame Turret

# Description __

Automated Flame turret. Requires Low Grade Fuel. Sprays flames when triggered.

Page views: 7,232  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Flashlight

# Description __

A powerful flashlight which illuminates your surroundings and can be used as a weapon.

Page views: 4,616  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Floor grill

# Description __

A floor grill must be placed in floor frames. Perfect for placing above a large furnace.

Page views: 4,423  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Ladder Hatch

# Description __

A hatch that opens and changes into a ladder.

Page views: 4,056  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Fogger-3000

# Description __

A Fog machine which runs on low grade fuel. Can be set to fill an area with a dense fog or triggered by motion.

Page views: 6,974  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Fridge

# Description __

A fridge you can store food into!

## Crafting Costs __

  * x75 Metal Fragments



## Recycling Output __

  * x38 Metal Fragments

# Shovel Bass

# Description __

Use this stringed together shovel to play some deep, deep tunes.

Page views: 3,599  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Cowbell

# Description __

A road sign that's been repurposed to produce some beautiful, calming, percussion.

Page views: 3,332  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
